    <div style="page-break-after:always; width:595.3pt;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;font-variant:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman, Times, serif ;font-size:10pt;">
      <div style="padding:0pt;margin:0pt;font-family:calibri, arial, sans-serif;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;font-size:8pt;line-height:8pt;">&#8203;</div>
      <div style="margin-top:15.85pt;height:24pt;margin-left:68pt;width:456pt;">
        <div style="margin-top:17pt; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#160;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="margin-top:13.15pt;height:648pt;margin-left:56pt;width:480pt;">
        <div style="position:relative;text-align:center; width:480pt;">
          <img src="lg_amazoncom-bw.jpg" alt="[MISSING IMAGE: lg_amazoncom-bw.jpg]" height="56" width="279" >
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:19pt; text-align:center; width:480pt; line-height:14pt;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:-0.24pt;">1997 LETTER TO SHAREHOLDERS</font><font style="font-size:10pt;">&#8203;<font style="letter-spacing:-0.2pt;"> </font></font>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:2pt; text-align:center; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;font-weight:bold;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:-0.2pt;">(Reprinted from the 1997 Annual Report)</font><font style="font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:0.2pt;"> </font>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:10pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">To our shareholders: </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:10pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Amazon.com passed many milestones in 1997: by year-end, we had served more than 1.5&#160;million customers, yielding 838% revenue growth to $147.8&#160;million, and extended our market leadership despite aggressive competitive&#160;entry. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:10pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">But this is Day 1 for the Internet and, if we execute well, for Amazon.com. Today, online commerce saves customers money and precious time. Tomorrow, through personalization, online commerce will accelerate the very process of discovery. Amazon.com uses the Internet to create real value for its customers and, by doing so, hopes to create an enduring franchise, even in established and large markets. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:10pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We have a window of opportunity as larger players marshal the resources to pursue the online opportunity and as customers, new to purchasing online, are receptive to forming new relationships. The competitive landscape&#160;has continued to evolve at a fast pace. Many large players have moved online with credible offerings and have devoted substantial energy and resources to building awareness, traffic, and sales. Our goal is to move quickly to solidify and extend our current position while we begin to pursue the online commerce opportunities in&#160;other areas. We see substantial opportunity in the large markets we are targeting. This strategy is not without risk:&#160;it requires serious investment and crisp execution against established franchise leaders. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:12pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;font-style:italic;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;It&#8217;s All About the Long Term</font><font style="font-style:normal;letter-spacing:0.2pt;"> </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:6pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We believe that a fundamental measure of our success will be the shareholder value we create over the </font><font style="font-style:italic;letter-spacing:0.2pt;">long term</font><font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">. This value will be a direct result of our ability to extend and solidify our current market leadership position. The stronger our market leadership, the more powerful our economic model. Market leadership can translate directly to higher revenue, higher profitability, greater capital velocity, and correspondingly stronger returns on invested capital. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:10pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Our decisions have consistently reflected this focus. We first measure ourselves in terms of the metrics most indicative of our market leadership: customer and revenue growth, the degree to which our customers continue to purchase from us on a repeat basis, and the strength of our brand. We have invested and will continue to invest aggressively to expand and leverage our customer base, brand, and infrastructure as we move to establish an enduring franchise. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:10pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Because of our emphasis on the long term, we may make decisions and weigh tradeoffs differently than some&#160;companies. Accordingly, we want to share with you our fundamental management and decision-making approach so that you, our shareholders, may confirm that it is consistent with your investment philosophy: </font>
        </div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We will continue to focus relentlessly on our customers. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We will continue to make investment decisions in light of long-term market leadership considerations rather than short-term profitability considerations or short-term Wall Street reactions. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We will continue to measure our programs and the effectiveness of our investments analytically, to jettison&#160;those that do not provide acceptable returns, and to step up our investment in those that work best. We will continue to learn from both our successes and our failures. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
      </div>
      <div style="margin-top:3.85000000000002pt;margin-bottom:35.86pt;margin-left:68pt;width:456pt;">
        <div style="margin-top:5pt; text-align:center; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#160;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
      </div>
      <hr >
    </div>
    <div style="page-break-after:always; width:595.3pt;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;font-variant:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman, Times, serif ;font-size:10pt;">
      <div style="padding:0pt;margin:0pt;font-family:calibri, arial, sans-serif;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;font-size:8pt;line-height:8pt;">&#8203;</div>
      <div style="margin-top:15.85pt;height:24pt;margin-left:68pt;width:456pt;">
        <div style="margin-top:17pt; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#160;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="margin-top:16.15pt;height:648pt;margin-left:56pt;width:480pt;">
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We will make bold rather than timid investment decisions where we see a sufficient probability of gaining&#160;market leadership advantages. Some of these investments will pay off, others will not, and we will&#160;have learned another valuable lesson in either case. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">When forced to choose between optimizing the appearance of our GAAP accounting and maximizing the&#160;present value of future cash flows, we&#8217;ll take the cash flows. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We will share our strategic thought processes with you when we make bold choices (to the extent competitive&#160;pressures allow), so that you may evaluate for yourselves whether we are making rational long-term leadership investments. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We will work hard to spend wisely and maintain our lean culture. We understand the importance of continually reinforcing a cost-conscious culture, particularly in a business incurring net losses. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We will balance our focus on growth with emphasis on long-term profitability and capital management. At&#160;this stage, we choose to prioritize growth because we believe that scale is central to achieving the potential&#160;of our business model. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We will continue to focus on hiring and retaining versatile and talented employees, and continue to weight&#160;their compensation to stock options rather than cash. We know our success will be largely affected&#160;by&#160;our ability to attract and retain a motivated employee base, each of whom must think like, and&#160;therefore must actually be, an owner. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:10pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We aren&#8217;t so bold as to claim that the above is the &#8220;right&#8221; investment philosophy, but it&#8217;s ours, and we would&#160;be remiss if we weren&#8217;t clear in the approach we have taken and will continue to take. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:10pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">With this foundation, we would like to turn to a review of our business focus, our progress in 1997, and our outlook for the future. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:12pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;font-style:italic;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Obsess Over Customers</font><font style="font-style:normal;letter-spacing:0.2pt;"> </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:6pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">From the beginning, our focus has been on offering our customers compelling value. We realized that the Web was, and still is, the World Wide Wait. Therefore, we set out to offer customers something they simply could&#160;not get any other way, and began serving them with books. We brought them much more selection than was possible in a physical store (our store would now occupy 6 football fields), and presented it in a useful, easy-</font>
          <br >
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">to&#8209;search, and easy-to-browse format in a store open 365&#160;days a year, 24 hours a day. We maintained a dogged focus&#160;on improving the shopping experience, and in 1997 substantially enhanced our store. We now offer customers gift certificates, 1-Click</font><font style=" position:relative; bottom:4.25pt;font-size:7.5pt;letter-spacing:0.15pt;">SM</font><font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;"> shopping, and vastly more reviews, content, browsing options, and recommendation features. We dramatically lowered prices, further increasing customer value. Word of mouth remains the most powerful customer acquisition tool we have, and we are grateful for the trust our customers have&#160;placed in us. Repeat purchases and word of mouth have combined to make Amazon.com the market leader in online bookselling. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-left:20pt; margin-top:10pt; width:460pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">By many measures, Amazon.com came a long way in 1997: </font>
        </div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Sales grew from $15.7&#160;million in 1996 to $147.8&#160;million&#8201;&#8211;&#8201;an 838% increase. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Cumulative customer accounts grew from 180,000 to 1,510,000&#8201;&#8211;&#8201;a 738% increase. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">The&#160;percentage of orders from repeat customers grew from over 46% in the fourth quarter of 1996 to over&#160;58% in the same period in 1997. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">In terms of audience reach, per Media Metrix, our Web site went from a rank of 90th to within the </font>
          <br >
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">top 20. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We established long-term relationships with many important strategic partners, including America Online,&#160;Yahoo!, Excite, Netscape, GeoCities, AltaVista, @Home, and Prodigy. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
      </div>
      <div style="margin-top:3.85000000000002pt;margin-bottom:35.86pt;margin-left:68pt;width:456pt;">
        <div style="margin-top:5pt; text-align:center; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#160;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
      </div>
      <hr >
    </div>
    <div style=" width:595.3pt;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;font-variant:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman, Times, serif ;font-size:10pt;">
      <div style="padding:0pt;margin:0pt;font-family:calibri, arial, sans-serif;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;font-size:8pt;line-height:8pt;">&#8203;</div>
      <div style="margin-top:15.85pt;height:24pt;margin-left:68pt;width:456pt;">
        <div style="margin-top:17pt; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#160;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="margin-top:16.15pt;margin-left:56pt;width:480pt;">
        <div style="width:480pt; line-height:12pt;font-style:italic;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Infrastructure</font><font style="font-style:normal;letter-spacing:0.2pt;"> </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:4pt; width:480pt; line-height:11.5pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">During 1997, we worked hard to expand our business infrastructure to support these greatly increased traffic, sales, and service levels: </font>
        </div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:5.8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:5.8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Amazon.com&#8217;s employee base grew from 158 to 614, and we significantly strengthened our management&#160;team. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:5.81pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:5.81pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Distribution center capacity grew from 50,000 to 285,000 square feet, including a 70% expansion of our Seattle facilities and the launch of our second distribution center in Delaware in November. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:5.8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:5.8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Inventories rose to over 200,000 titles at year-end, enabling us to improve availability for our customers. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; margin-left:20pt; line-height:12pt; margin-top:5.8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:10pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#8226;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:5.8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:30pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Our cash and investment balances at year-end were $125&#160;million, thanks to our initial public offering in May&#160;1997 and our $75&#160;million loan, affording us substantial strategic flexibility. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style="margin-top:12pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;font-style:italic;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Employees</font><font style="font-style:normal;letter-spacing:0.2pt;"> </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:4pt; width:480pt; line-height:11.5pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">The past year&#8217;s success is the product of a talented, smart, hard-working group, and I take great pride in being a part of this team. Setting the bar high in our approach to hiring has been, and will continue to be, the single most important element of Amazon.com&#8217;s success. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:10pt; width:480pt; line-height:11.5pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">It&#8217;s not easy to work here (when I interview people I tell them, &#8220;You can work long, hard, or smart, but at Amazon.com you can&#8217;t choose two out of three&#8221;), but we are working to build something important, something that matters to our customers, something that we can all tell our grandchildren about. Such things aren&#8217;t meant to be easy. We are incredibly fortunate to have this group of dedicated employees whose sacrifices and passion build Amazon.com. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:12pt; width:480pt; line-height:12pt;font-style:italic;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Goals for 1998</font><font style="font-style:normal;letter-spacing:0.2pt;"> </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:4pt; width:480pt; line-height:11.5pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We are still in the early stages of learning how to bring new value to our customers through Internet commerce and merchandising. Our goal remains to continue to solidify and extend our brand and customer base. This requires sustained investment in systems and infrastructure to support outstanding customer convenience, selection, and service while we grow. We are planning to add music to our product offering, and over time we believe&#160;that other products may be prudent investments. We also believe there are significant opportunities to better&#160;serve our customers overseas, such as reducing delivery times and better tailoring the customer experience. To be certain, a big part of the challenge for us will lie not in finding new ways to expand our business, but in prioritizing our investments. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:10pt; width:480pt; line-height:11.5pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We now know vastly more about online commerce than when Amazon.com was founded, but we still have so&#160;much to learn. Though we are optimistic, we must remain vigilant and maintain a sense of urgency. The challenges and hurdles we will face to make our long-term vision for Amazon.com a reality are several: aggressive,&#160;capable, well-funded competition; considerable growth challenges and execution risk; the risks of product and geographic expansion; and the need for large continuing investments to meet an expanding market opportunity. However, as we&#8217;ve long said, online bookselling, and online commerce in general, should prove to be&#160;a&#160;very large market, and it&#8217;s likely that a number of companies will see significant benefit. We feel good about what we&#8217;ve done, and even more excited about what we want to do. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="text-indent:20pt; margin-top:10pt; width:480pt; line-height:11.5pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">1997 was indeed an incredible year. We at Amazon.com are grateful to our customers for their business and trust, to each other for our hard work, and to our shareholders for their support and encouragement. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="position:relative;margin-left:240pt; margin-top:17.9pt; width:240pt;">
          <img src="sg_jeffreypbezos-bw.jpg" alt="[MISSING IMAGE: sg_jeffreypbezos-bw.jpg]" height="61" width="175" >
        </div>
        <div style="margin-left:240pt; margin-top:14.8pt; width:240pt; line-height:11.5pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Jeffrey P. Bezos </font>
          <br >
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Founder and Chief Executive Officer </font>
          <br >
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Amazon.com, Inc.</font>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="margin-top:3.85000000000002pt;margin-bottom:35.86pt;margin-left:68pt;width:456pt;">
        <div style="margin-top:5pt; text-align:center; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#160;</font>
          <br >
        </div>

    <div style="page-break-after:always; width:595.3pt;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;font-variant:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman, Times, serif ;font-size:10pt;">
      <div style="padding:0pt;margin:0pt;font-family:calibri, arial, sans-serif;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;font-size:8pt;line-height:8pt;">&#8203;</div>
      <div style="margin-top:15.85pt;height:24pt;margin-left:68pt;width:456pt;">
        <div style="margin-top:17pt; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#160;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="margin-top:16.15pt;height:648pt;margin-left:68pt;width:456pt;">
        <div style="text-align:right; width:456pt;font-weight:bold;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:-0.2pt;">&#8202;Exhibit&#160;99.2</font>
          <br >
          <font style="letter-spacing:-0.2pt;">&#8202;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font>&#8203;</div>
        <div style="width:456pt; line-height:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:-0.2pt;">Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Financial Measures</font><font style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:0.2pt;"> </font>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:8pt; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Our measures of free cash flows and the effect of foreign exchange rates on our consolidated statements of operations meet the definition of non-GAAP financial measures. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:8pt; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">We provide multiple measures of free cash flows because we believe these measures provide additional perspective on the impact of acquiring property and equipment with cash and through finance leases and financing obligations. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:8pt; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Free cash flow is cash flow from operations reduced by &#8220;Purchases of property and equipment, net of proceeds from sales and incentives.&#8221; Free cash flow less principal repayments of finance leases and financing obligations is free cash flow reduced by &#8220;Principal repayments of finance leases&#8221; and &#8220;Principal repayments of financing obligations.&#8221; </font>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:8pt; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Free cash flow adjusted for equipment finance leases, which we also refer to as free cash flow less equipment finance leases and principal repayments of all other finance leases and financing obligations, is free cash flow reduced by equipment acquired under finance leases, which is included in &#8220;Property and equipment acquired under finance leases, net of remeasurements and modifications,&#8221; principal repayments of all other finance lease liabilities, which is included in &#8220;Principal repayments of finance leases,&#8221; and &#8220;Principal repayments of financing obligations.&#8221; All other finance lease liabilities and financing obligations consists of property. In this measure, equipment acquired under finance leases is reflected as if these assets had been purchased with cash, which is not the case as these assets have been leased. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:8pt; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">These free cash flows measures have limitations as they omit certain components of the overall cash flow statement and do not represent the residual cash flow available for discretionary expenditures. For example, these measures of free cash flows do not incorporate the portion of payments representing principal reductions of debt or cash payments for business acquisitions. Additionally, our mix of property and equipment acquisitions with cash or other financing options may change over time. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flows measures only as a complement to our entire consolidated statements of cash flows. </font>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:8pt; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">A quantitative reconciliation of free cash flow adjusted for equipment finance leases to the most directly comparable amounts reported in accordance with GAAP for the trailing twelve&#160;months ended December&#160;31, 2023 and 2024, is set forth below. </font>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="margin-top:3.85000000000002pt;margin-bottom:35.86pt;margin-left:68pt;width:456pt;">
        <div style="margin-top:5pt; text-align:center; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#160;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
      </div>
      <hr >
    </div>
    <div style=" width:595.3pt;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;font-variant:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman, Times, serif ;font-size:10pt;">
      <div style="padding:0pt;margin:0pt;font-family:calibri, arial, sans-serif;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;font-size:8pt;line-height:8pt;">&#8203;</div>
      <div style="margin-top:15.85pt;height:24pt;margin-left:68pt;width:456pt;">
        <div style="margin-top:17pt; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">&#160;</font>
          <br >
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="margin-top:16.15pt;height:648pt;margin-left:68pt;width:456pt;">
        <div style="text-align:center; width:456pt; line-height:12pt;font-weight:bold;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:-0.2pt;">AMAZON.COM, INC. </font>
          <br >
          <font style="letter-spacing:-0.2pt;">(in millions) </font>

          <font style="letter-spacing:-0.2pt;">(unaudited)</font><font style="font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:0.2pt;"> </font>

          <tr style="line-height:9pt;white-space:nowrap;text-align:center;vertical-align:bottom;font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-variant:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman, Times, serif ;font-size:8pt;">

            <td style="padding:0pt;border-bottom:1px solid #FFFFFF; width:6pt;">&#8203;</td>

        </div>

        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; line-height:12pt; margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:20pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">(3)</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:20pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Free cash flow is cash flow from operations reduced by &#8220;Purchases of property and equipment, net of proceeds from sales and incentives.&#8221; </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; line-height:12pt; margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:20pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">(4)</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:20pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Free cash flow less principal repayments of finance leases and financing obligations is free cash flow reduced by &#8220;Principal repayments of finance leases&#8221; and &#8220;Principal repayments of financing obligations.&#8221; </font>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:both; padding:0pt; margin:0pt;font-size:0pt;line-height:0pt;">&#8203;</div>
        <div style=" float:left; line-height:12pt; margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:left; width:20pt;white-space:nowrap;">
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">(5)</font>
          <br >
        </div>
        <div style=" margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:12pt; text-align:left; margin-left:20pt;">
          <!--blacklining:none;-->
          <font style="letter-spacing:0.2pt;">Free cash flow less equipment finance leases and principal repayments of all other finance leases and financing obligations is free cash flow reduced by equipment acquired under finance leases, which is included in &#8220;Property and equipment acquired under finance leases, net of remeasurements and modifications,&#8221; principal repayments of all other finance lease liabilities, which is included in &#8220;Principal repayments of finance leases,&#8221; and &#8220;Principal repayments of financing obligations.&#8221;</font>
        </div>
